 jab yojana ayog ko yah maansik vilaas karne kaa sarkari adhikaar he to hamane aisa kya bigaada he ki ham garib par baat na karen?aamtaur par yah mana jaataa he ki aadmi do tarah ke hote hai-garib aadmi, or amir aadmi
 Wise people like us believe that this classification is wrong
 isamen garib ko aadmi maanakar chalaa ja rahaa he
 This is not right garib ko aadmi maanane par amir naaraaz hote hai
 a sensitive government can also be angry
 garib ko aadmi kaho to kehane vaale ko naksali qaraar diya ja saktaa he

 use aadmi kehane, na kehane kaa nirnay aap par chhodte hai

 kuch log maanate hai ki jo amir nahin he, vah automatic hi garib he

 sara pech use aadmi maanane na maanane kaa he

 uski bhi do taangen, do haath, gardan, sir tathaa pet hota he

 varanaa iskaa sir bhi hota he go ki vah pet ke chakkar main itnaa jhukaa rahata he ki dikhataa hi nahin

 isaki do taangen bhi hoti hai

 garib ke do haath bhi hote hai
 These are always empty
 garib ke sir par ek adad suunaa aasmaan tana rahata he, jisamen un toton ke alaava or koi nahin hota jo garib ke haathon se ude hote hai

 ye itani khaali hoti hai ki unamem jhaankne se bhi dar lagata he

 unase use jamaane bhar kii laanatein tathaa gaaliyaan sunne kii ishwar pradutt suvidha mili hoti he

 garibi hi uskaa puraa samay le leti he

 garib is dharti kaa sabase purana praani he

 garibi, amiri kaa vilom katai nahin he

 ab bachaa itihaas

 is seat par 11 april ko matdaan he
 Political Background: The history of Amalapuram Lok Sabha seat is very interesting
 is seat par shuruaati do aam chunaavon (1952 or 1957 loksabhaa chunaav) ko jeetne vaali communist party of india (CPI) vartmaan main apane vajood kii ladaai lard rahi he
 At the same time, the Congress, which had won 5 consecutive general elections before 1982, suffered a major setback with the coming of TDP and its vote fell significantly
 tidipi kaa gathan 1982 main hua or iske baad hue 9 aam chunaavon main congress ko 4 baar hi kamyaabi mil saki
 At the same time, TDP has won the victory 5 times
 is seat par 1984 main tidipi, 1989 main congress, 1991 main tidipi, 1996 main congress, 1998 or 1999 main tidipi, 2004 or 2009 main congress ne jeet darj kii
 At the same time, TDP, which contested in 2014 in alliance with Modi wave, won here
 saamaajik taana-banaarakshit loksabhaa seat amalapuram kii adhiktar janata gaanvon main basati he
 Most people here are farmers
 18 lakh 72 hajaar se zyada kii jansankhya vaale is loksabhaa kshetra main 91 fisadi log gaanvon main rahete hai or kareeb 9 fisadi logon ne hi shahar kii ore rukh kiya he

 Pakistan's newly elected Prime Minister Imran Khan's cabinet was sworn in on Monday
 in mantriyon ke bharose imran 'nayaa pakistan' banane kaa daawa kar rahe hai, lekin sachai yah he ki unki cabinet main aadhe se zyaadaamantrivahi hai jo paravejamusharrafke kaarykaal main mantri rah chuke hai
 According to Pakistani newspaper The News, there are 12 ministers in the Pakistan tehreek-e-insaf (PTI) government who have been ministers in the former General (retired) Pervez Musharraf government
 inamen kai ko lene kii vajah unki varishthata or anubhav ko bataaya ja rahaa he
 Imran's 21-member Council of Ministers includes former spokesperson of Pervez Musharraf, his former attorney and several ministers in Musharraf's Council of Ministers
 sabase mahatvapurn baat yah he ki in sabhi mantriyon ko kaaphi mahatvapurn vibhaag bhi mili hai
 These are the leaders of the new minister Musharraf's era, Farogh Naseem (minister of Law and Justice), Tariq Bashir Cheema (state and Frontier Region), Ghulam Sarwar Khan (petroleum), Zubaida Jalal (defense Production), Fawad Chaudhary (information and Broadcasting), Sheikh Rashid Ahmed (rail), Khalid Maqbool Siddiqui (IT & Telecom), Shafaqat Mahmood (education & Professional Training), Maqdoom Khusro Bakhtiar (water Resources), Abdul Razak Dawood (commerce, Textiles a A
 Industry), Dr
 ishrat hossain (sansthagat sudhaar), or amin asalam (jalwaayu parivartan), shaamil hai
 There are five ministers in the new cabinet who have also been ministers in the Pakistan People's Party government
 inamen parvej khataak (raksha), babar awan (sansadeey maamle), shah mahmud kuraishi (videsh), fahmida mirza (prantiy samanvay), or fawaad choudhary (soochna evam prasaaran) shaamil hai
 PTI veterans have got only three departments of the cabinet
 inamen asad umr (vitt evam rajasav), shirin majaari (maanavadhikaar) or aamir kiyani (swasthya) shaamil hai
 Significantly, the President of Pakistan, Mamnoon Hussain administered the oath of office to Imran Khan on 18 August
 iske baad somvaar, 20 agast ko raashtrapati bhawan main 16 cabinet mantriyon ne shapath lee

 The Indian Railway Catering and Tourism Corporation (IRCTC) will start a rail-based weekly travel package from November 21, so that travelers seeking to save time travel on three historic and vibrant cities - Delhi, Agra and Jaipur - the Golden Triangle - with three Shatabdi Express trains
 Will be able to do it
 dilli se agra or jaipur kii do din kii rail yatra package pahal ke tahat teen shatabdi express trainon ke tikat aapas main jod die gaye hai, taaki yatriyon ko ek aaraamdeh evam pareshaani mukt yatra kaarykram uplabdh karaayaa ja sake
 IRCTC chief and managing director AK Manocha said, "it is one of those innovative travel packages that is perfectly suited for travelers planning short-haul travel
" package se yatri desh ke kuch sabase prasiddh smarakon kii bhavyata kaa anubhav kar sakate hai
 Shatabdi trains are one of the fastest trains on the Indian rail network and food is also provided in these air-conditioned trains
 package har shanivaar or ravivaar ke liye he or 21 november se shuru hoga
 Guests will board the delhi-habibganj Shatabdi and leave the train at Agra in the early hours of a two-day 'golden Triangle Package' at New Delhi station
 package ke tahat yatriyon ko agra kaa tajmahal, itmaad ud daula kaa makbara, agra kila dikhaaya jayega or shahar ke ek paanch sitara hotel main dopaher kaa bhojan karaayaa jayega
 After this, they will reach Jaipur in the morning riding in agra-jaipur Shatabdi
 tippaniyan They will also be visited famous places in Jaipur
 or vahaan se ve jaipur-nayi dilli shatabdi express main savaar hokar dilli laut aaenge
 They will be taken in air-conditioned trains to all destinations
 do yatriyon ke saath hone par package kii prati vyakti laagat 9,444 rupee he or isamen smarakon kaa pravesh shulk shaamil nahin he
 The booking of the package can be done on the tourism portal of IRCTC
 adhik jaankaree ke liye 1800110139 par phone kiya ja saktaa he, joki ek toll free number he
 The tickets for the three Shatabdi Express trains have been added as part of the two-day rail travel package initiative from Delhi to Agra and Jaipur, to provide a comfortable and hassle-free itinerary to the passengers
 iarsitisi ke pramukh or prabandh nideshak eke manocha ne kaha, yah un abhinav yatra packejon main se ek he, jo kam samay ke safar kii yojana banane vaale yatriyon ke puri tarah anukool he
 With the package, travelers can experience the grandeur of some of the most famous monuments in the country
 shatabdi trainen bhartiya rail network kii sabase tej raftaar vaali trainon main se ek hai or in vaataanukoolit trainon main bhojan bhi uplabdh karaayaa jaataa he
 The package is for every Saturday and Sunday and will start on 21 November
 ek raat-do din ke 'golden triengal package' ke tahat nai dilli stesan par tadake mehmaan dilli-habibganj shatabdi main savaar honge or agra main train chodenge
 As part of the package, passengers will be shown the Taj Mahal of Agra, the tomb of Itmad ud Daulah, Agra Fort and will be served lunch at a five-star hotel in the city
 iske baad ve agra-jaipur shatabdi main savaar hokar subah jaipur pahunchenge

 And from there, he will return to Delhi by boarding the jaipur-new Delhi Shatabdi Express
 sabhi sthalon ke liye unhen vaataanukoolit gadiyon main le jaaya jayega
 The per person cost of the package, with two passengers, is Rs 9,444 and does not include the entrance fee for the monuments

 Hartalika Teej Vrat is celebrated as the festival of the reunion of Lord Shiva and Maramparvati
 isliye har stri ke liye yevratvishesh laabhakaari mana gaya he
 Today, we will tell you everything related to this fasting, which will make your fast even more auspicious and fruitful
 haratalika teej kab he?paavan vrath haratalika teej bhadrapada maas ke shukla paksh kii tritiya tithi ko kiya jaataa he
 Worshiping Lord Shiva and Goddess Parvati in Hast Nakshatra on Shukla Tritiya of Bhadrapada has special significance
 is baar haratalika teej kavrat12 sitanbaryani kal he
 Importance of Hartalika Teej - This fast is also called Haritalika Teej and also Haratalika Teej
 - is vrath kaa sambandhbhagavanshiv se he
 - 'hara' is the name of Shiva, hence the name of this fast is considered to be more appropriate
 - bhadrapada shukla kii tritiya tithi ko manaaya jaataa he haratalika teej kaa parv, is din mahilaayein nirjal vrath rakhane kaa sankalp leti hai
 - Mainly this festival is kept for wishing a desired and worthy husband
 haalanki koi bhi stri ye vrath ko rakh sakati he
 - This time Haritalika Teej will be celebrated on 12 September
 kyon khaas he haratalika teej vrath-is vrath ko lekar manyata ye bhi he ki bhagwaan shiv ko pati rup main paane ke liema parvatine varshon tak jangal main ghor tapasya kii
 After meditating without water and without food, she was accepted as a consort by Lord Shiva
 isliye haritalika teej ke din mahilaayein nishtha or tapasya ko vishesh mahatv detii hai

 lekin sehat thik naa ho to falahar par bhi vrath rakh sakate hai
 - In the evening, worship Lord Shiva and Parvati jointly, keep in mind that during worship, women should remain in complete adornment
 - iske baad maa parvati ko saubhaahgya kii vasteen arpit karen or unase apni manokamana kii purti ke liye prarthana karen
 - Married women should take blessings from their mother-in-law on this day by giving them items of good fortune

 - Since the year 2015, there is talk about the deal of this missile system in india-russia

 lekin vishwa kaa sirf 4 fisadi saaf pani hi desh main he
